getRandom(prefix) {\n    return prefix + Math.random().toString().slice(2);\n}\n\n// ÊõøÊç¢ html ÁâπÊÆäÂ≠óÁ¨¶\nfunction replaceHtmlSymbol(html) {\n    if (html == null) {\n        return '';\n    }\n    return html.replace(/</gm, '&lt;').replace(/>/gm, '&gt;').replace(/\"/gm, '&quot;').replace(/(\\r\\n|\\r|\\n)/g, '<br/>');\n}\n\n// ËøîÂõûÁôæÂàÜÊØîÁöÑÊ†ºÂºè\n\n\n// Âà§Êñ≠ÊòØ‰∏çÊòØ var pasteText = void 0;\n    if (clipboardData == null) {\n        pasteText = window.clipboardData && window.clipboardData.getData('text');\n    } else {\n        pasteText = clipboardData.getData('text/plain');\n    }\n\n    return replaceHtmlSymbol(pasteText);\n}\n\n// Ëé∑ÂèñÁ≤òË¥¥ÁöÑhtml\nfunction getPasteHtml(e, filterStyle, ignoreImg) {\n    var clipboardData = e.clipboardData || e.originalEvent && e.originalEvent.clipboardData;\n    var pasteText = void 0,\n        pasteHtml = void 0;\n    if (clipboardData == null) {\n        pasteText = window.clipboardData && window.clipboardData.getData('text');\n    } else {\n        pasteText = clipboardData.getData('text/plain');\n        pasteHtml = clipboardData.getData('text/html');\n    }\n    if (!pasteHtml && pasteText) {\n        pasteHtml = '<p>' + replaceHtmlSymbol(pasteText) + '</p>';\n    }\n    if (!pasteHtml) {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    // ËøáÊª§word‰∏≠Áä∂ÊÄÅËøáÊù•ÁöÑÊó†Áî®Â≠óÁ¨¶\n    var docSplitHtml = pasteHtml.split('</html>');\n    if (docSplitHtml.length === 2) {\n        pasteHtml = docSplitHtml[0];\n    }\n\n    // ËøáÊª§Êó†Áî®Ê†áÁ≠æ\n    pasteHtml = pasteHtml.replace(/<(meta|script|link).+?>/igm, '');\n    // ÂéªÊéâÊ≥®Èáä\n    pasteHtml = pasteHtml.replace(/<!--.*?-->/mg, '');\n    // ËøáÊª§ data-xxx Â±ûÊÄß\n    pasteHtml = pasteHtml.replace(/\\s?data-.+?=('|\").+?('|\")/igm, '');\n\n    if (ignoreImg) {\n        // ÂøΩÁï•ÂõæÁâá\n        pasteHtml = pasteHtml.replace(/<img.+?>/igm, '');\n    }\n\n    if (filterStyle) {\n        // ËøáÊª§Ê†∑Âºè\n        pasteHtml = pasteHtml.replace(/\\s?(class|style)=('|\").*?('|\")/igm, '');\n    } else {\n        // ‰øùÁïôÊ†∑Âºè\n        pasteHtml = pasteHtml.replace(/\\s?class=('|\").*?('|\")/igm, '');\n    }\n\n    return pasteHtml;\n}\n\n// Ëé∑ÂèñÁ≤òË¥¥ÁöÑÂõæÁâáÊñá‰ª∂\nfunction getPasteImgs(e) {\n    var result = [];\n    var txt = getPasteText(e);\n    if (txt) {\n        // ÊúâÊñáÂ≠óÔºåÂ∞±ÂøΩÁï•ÂõæÁâá\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    var clipboardData = e.clipboardData || e.originalEvent && e.originalEvent.clipboardData || {};\n    var items = clipboardData.items;\n    if (!items) {\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    objForEach(items, function (key, value) {\n        var type = value.type;\n        if (/image/i.test(type)) {\n            result.push(value.getAsFile());\n        }\n    });\n\n    return result;\n}\n\n/*\n    ÁºñËæëÂå∫Âüü\n*/\n\n// Ëé∑Âèñ‰∏Ä‰∏™ elem.childNodes ÁöÑ JSON Êï∞ÊçÆ\nfunction getChildrenJSON($elem) {\n    var result = [];\n    var $children = $elem.childNodes() || []; // Ê≥®ÊÑè childNodes() ÂèØ‰ª•Ëé∑ÂèñÊñáÊú¨ËäÇÁÇπ\n    $children.forEach(function (curElem) elemResult = replaceHtmlSymbol(elemResult);\n        }\n\n        // ÊôÆÈÄö DOM ËäÇÁÇπ\n        if (nodeType === 1) {\n            elemResult = {};\n\n            // tag\n            elemResult.tag = curElem.nodeName.toLowerCase();\n            // attr\n            var attrData = [];\n            var attrList = curElem.attributes || {};\n            var attrListLength = attrList.length || 0;\n            for (var i = 0; i < attrListLength; i++) {\n                var attr = attrList[i];\n                attrData.push({\n                    name: attr.name,\n                    value: attr.value\n                });\n            }\n            elemResult.attrs = attrData;\n            // childrenÔºàÈÄíÂΩíÔºâ\n            elemResult.children = getChildrenJSON($(curElem));\n        }\n\n        result.push(elemResult);\n    });\n    return result;\n}\n\n// ÊûÑÈÄ†ÂáΩÊï∞\nfunction Text(editor) {\n    this.editor = editor;\n}\n\n// ‰øÆÊîπÂéüÂûã\nText.prototype = {\n    constructor: // ÊåâÂõûËΩ¶ÈîÆÊó∂ÁöÑÁâπÊÆäÂ§ÑÁêÜ\n    _enterKeyHandle: function _enterKeyHandle() {\n        var editor = this.editor;\n        var $textElem = editor.$textElem;\n\n        function    e.preventDefault();\n            }\n\n            // Á≤òË¥¥ÂõæÁâáÂíåÊñáÊú¨ÔºåÂè™ËÉΩÂêåÊó∂‰ΩøÁî®‰∏Ä‰∏™\n            if (!canDo()) {\n                return;\n            }\n\n            //    var editor = this.editor;\n        var $textElem = editor.$textElem;\n\n        $textElem.on('keydown', function (e) {\n            if (e.keyCode !== 9) {\n                return;\n            }\n   _dragHandle: function _dragHandle() {\n        var editor = this.editor;\n\n        // Á¶ÅÁî® document ÊãñÊãΩ‰∫ã‰ª∂\n        var $document = $(document);\n        $document.on('dragleave drop ÊûÑÈÄ†ÂáΩÊï∞\nfunction Command(editor) {\n    this.editor = editor;\n}\n\n// ‰øÆÊîπÂéüÂûã\nCommand.prototype = {\n    constructor: Command,\n\n    // ÊâßË°åÂëΩ‰ª§\n    do: function _do(name, value) {\n        var editor = this.editor;\n\n        // ‰ΩøÁî® styleWithCSS\n        if (!editor._useStyleWithCSS) {\n            document.execCommand('styleWithCSS', null, true);\n            editor._useStyleWithCSS = true;\n        }\n\n        // Â¶ÇÊûúÊó†ÈÄâÂå∫ÔºåÂøΩÁï•\n        if (!editor.selection.getRange()) {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // ÊÅ¢Â§çÈÄâÂèñ\n        editor.selection.restoreSelection();\n\n        // ÊâßË°å\n        var _name = '_' + name;\n        if (this[_name]) {\n            // ÊúâËá™ÂÆö‰πâ‰∫ã‰ª∂\n            this[_name](value);\n        } else {\n            // ÈªòËÆ§ command\n            this._execCommand(name, value);\n        }\n\n        // ‰øÆÊîπËèúÂçïÁä∂ÊÄÅ\n        editor.menus.changeActive();\n\n        // ÊúÄÂêéÔºåÊÅ¢Â§çÈÄâÂèñ‰øùËØÅÂÖâÊ†áÂú®ÂéüÊù•ÁöÑ‰ΩçÁΩÆÈó™ÁÉÅ\n        editor.selection.saveRange();\n        editor.selection.restoreSelection();\n\n        // Ëß¶Âèë onchange\n        editor.change && editor.change();\n    },\n\n    // Ëá™ÂÆö‰πâ insertHTML ‰∫ã‰ª∂\n    _insertHTML: function _insertHTML(html) {\n        var editor = this.editor;\n        var range = editor.selection.getRange();\n\n        if (this.queryCommandSupported('insertHTML')) {\n            // W3C\n            this._execCommand('insertHTML', html);\n        } else if (range.insertNode) {\n            // IE\n            range.deleteContents();\n            range.insertNode($(html)[0]);\n        } else if (range.pasteHTML) {\n            // IE <= 10\n            range.pasteHTML(html);\n        }\n    },\n\n    // ÊèíÂÖ• elem\n    _insertElem: function _insertElem($elem) {\n        var editor = this.editor;\n        var range = editor.selection.getRange();\n\n        if (range.insertNode) {\n            range.deleteContents();\n            range.insertNode($elem[0]);\n        }\n    },\n\n    // Â∞ÅË£Ö execCommand\n    _execCommand: function _execCommand(name, value) {\n        document.execCommand(name, false, value);\n    },\n\n    // Â∞ÅË£Ö document.queryCommandValue\n    queryCommandValue: function queryCommandValue(name) {\n        return document.queryCommandValue(name);\n    },\n\n    // Â∞ÅË£Ö document.queryCommandState\n    queryCommandState: function queryCommandState(name) {\n        return document.queryCommandState(name);\n    },\n\n    // Â∞ÅË£Ö document.queryCommandSupported\n    queryCommandSupported: function queryCommandSupported(name) {\n        return document.queryCommandSupported(name);\n    }\n};\n\n/*\n    selection range API\n*/\n\n// ÊûÑÈÄ†ÂáΩÊï∞\nfunction API(editor) {\n    this.editor = editor;\n    this._currentRange = null;\n}\n\n// ‰øÆÊîπÂéüÂûã\nAPI.prototype = {\n    constructor: API,\n\n    // Ëé∑Âèñ range ÂØπË±°\n    getRange: function getRange() {\n        return this._currentRange;\n    },\n\n    // ‰øùÂ≠òÈÄâÂå∫\n    saveRange: function saveRange(_range) {\n        if (_range) {\n            // ‰øùÂ≠òÂ∑≤ÊúâÈÄâÂå∫\n            this._currentRange = _range;\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Ëé∑ÂèñÂΩìÂâçÁöÑÈÄâÂå∫\n        var selection = window.getSelection();\n        if (selection.rangeCount === 0) {\n            return;\n        }\n        var range = selection.getRangeAt(0);\n\n        // Âà§Êñ≠ÈÄâÂå∫ÂÜÖÂÆπÊòØÂê¶Âú®ÁºñËæëÂÜÖÂÆπ‰πãÂÜÖ\n        var $containerElem =               _this.isFocus = false;\n                } else {\n                    if (!_this.isFocus) {\n                        _this.onfocus && _this.onfocus();\n                    }\n                    _this.isFocus = true;\n                }\n            });\n        }\n    },\n\n    // Â∞ÅË£Ö command\n    _initCommand: function _initCommand() {\n        this.cmd = new Command(this);\n 'function') {\n            this.onfocus = function () {\n                onfocus();\n            };\n        }\n    },\n\n    // ÂàõÂª∫ÁºñËæëÂô®\n    create: function create() {\n        //
